-- insert into table

declare @StartValue int;
set @StartValue=(select last_num from new_num where table_name = 'pr_emp_rent_details');

insert into pr_emp_rent_details(id,[fy],[fm],[emp_id],[emp_code],[rent_mid],[amount],[active],[trans_id]) 
select @StartValue+ROW_NUMBER() OVER(ORDER BY emp_code) AS Row,[fy],[fm],[emp_id],[emp_code],[rent_mid],[amount],[active],[trans_id] from pr_emp_rent_details_temp

declare @lastnum int;
set @lastnum = (select top 1 id from pr_emp_rent_details order by id desc)
update new_num set last_num=@lastnum where table_name='pr_emp_rent_details'


--drop 

 drop table pr_emp_rent_details_temp
